    85	function gsdHome(): string {
    86	  return process.env.GSD_HOME || join(homedir(), ".gsd");
    87	}

    89	function globalPreferencesPath(): string {
    90	  return join(gsdHome(), "preferences.md");

    94	  return join(homedir(), ".pi", "agent", "gsd-preferences.md");

    98	  return join(gsdRoot(process.cwd()), "preferences.md");

   100	// Bootstrap in gitignore.ts historically created PREFERENCES.md (uppercase) by mistake.
   101	// Check uppercase as a fallback so those files aren't silently ignored.
   102	function globalPreferencesPathUppercase(): string {
   103	  return join(gsdHome(), "PREFERENCES.md");
   104	}
   105	function projectPreferencesPathUppercase(): string {
   106	  return join(gsdRoot(process.cwd()), "PREFERENCES.md");
   107	}

   110	  return globalPreferencesPath();
   111	}

   121	// ─── Loading ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   122	
   123	export function loadGlobalGSDPreferences(): LoadedGSDPreferences | null {
   124	  return loadPreferencesFile(globalPreferencesPath(), "global")
   125	    ?? loadPreferencesFile(globalPreferencesPathUppercase(), "global")
   126	    ?? loadPreferencesFile(legacyGlobalPreferencesPath(), "global");
   127	}
   128	
   129	export function loadProjectGSDPreferences(): LoadedGSDPreferences | null {
   130	  return loadPreferencesFile(projectPreferencesPath(), "project")
   131	    ?? loadPreferencesFile(projectPreferencesPathUppercase(), "project");
   132	}
   133	
   134	export function loadEffectiveGSDPreferences(): LoadedGSDPreferences | null {
   135	  const globalPreferences = loadGlobalGSDPreferences();
   136	  const projectPreferences = loadProjectGSDPreferences();
   137	
   138	  if (!globalPreferences && !projectPreferences) return null;
   139	
   140	  let result: LoadedGSDPreferences;
   141	  if (!globalPreferences) {
   142	    result = projectPreferences!;
   143	  } else if (!projectPreferences) {
   144	    result = globalPreferences;
   145	  } else {
   146	    const mergedWarnings = [
   147	      ...(globalPreferences.warnings ?? []),
   148	      ...(projectPreferences.warnings ?? []),
   149	    ];
   150	    result = {
   151	      path: projectPreferences.path,
   152	      scope: "project",
   153	      preferences: mergePreferences(globalPreferences.preferences, projectPreferences.preferences),
   154	      ...(mergedWarnings.length > 0 ? { warnings: mergedWarnings } : {}),
   155	    };
   156	  }
   157	
   158	  // Apply token-profile defaults as the lowest-priority layer so that
   159	  // `token_profile: budget` sets models and phase-skips automatically.
   160	  // Explicit user preferences always override profile defaults.
   161	  const profile = result.preferences.token_profile as TokenProfile | undefined;
   162	  if (profile) {
   163	    const profileDefaults = _resolveProfileDefaults(profile);
   164	    result = {
   165	      ...result,
   166	      preferences: mergePreferences(profileDefaults as GSDPreferences, result.preferences),
   167	    };
   168	  }
   169	
   170	  // Apply mode defaults as the lowest-priority layer
   171	  if (result.preferences.mode) {
   172	    result = {
   173	      ...result,
   174	      preferences: applyModeDefaults(result.preferences.mode, result.preferences),
   175	    };
   176	  }
   177	
   178	  return result;
   179	}
   180	
   181	function loadPreferencesFile(path: string, scope: "global" | "project"): LoadedGSDPreferences | null {
   182	  if (!existsSync(path)) return null;
   183	
   184	  const raw = readFileSync(path, "utf-8");
   185	  const preferences = parsePreferencesMarkdown(raw);
   186	  if (!preferences) return null;
   187	
   188	  const validation = validatePreferences(preferences);
   189	  const allWarnings = [...validation.warnings, ...validation.errors];
   190	
   191	  return {
   192	    path,
   193	    scope,
   194	    preferences: validation.preferences,
   195	    ...(allWarnings.length > 0 ? { warnings: allWarnings } : {}),
   196	  };
   197	}
   198	
   199	let _warnedUnrecognizedFormat = false;
   200	
   201	/** @internal Reset the warn-once flag — exported for testing only. */
   202	export function _resetParseWarningFlag(): void {
   203	  _warnedUnrecognizedFormat = false;
   204	}
   205	
   206	/** @internal Exported for testing only */
   207	export function parsePreferencesMarkdown(content: string): GSDPreferences | null {
   208	  // Use indexOf instead of [\s\S]*? regex to avoid backtracking (#468)
   209	  const startMarker = content.startsWith('---\r\n') ? '---\r\n' : '---\n';
   210	  if (content.startsWith(startMarker)) {
   211	    const searchStart = startMarker.length;
   212	    const endIdx = content.indexOf('\n---', searchStart);
   213	    if (endIdx === -1) return null;
   214	    const block = content.slice(searchStart, endIdx);
   215	    return parseFrontmatterBlock(block.replace(/\r/g, ''));
   216	  }
   217	
   218	  // Fallback: heading+list format (e.g. "## Git\n- isolation: none") (#2036)
   219	  // GSD agents may write preferences files without frontmatter delimiters.
   220	  if (/^##\s+\w/m.test(content)) {
   221	    return parseHeadingListFormat(content);
   222	  }
   223	
   224	  if (!_warnedUnrecognizedFormat) {
   225	    _warnedUnrecognizedFormat = true;
   226	    console.warn("[parsePreferencesMarkdown] preferences.md exists but uses an unrecognized format — skipping.");
   227	  }
   228	  return null;
   229	}
   230	
   231	function parseFrontmatterBlock(frontmatter: string): GSDPreferences {
   232	  try {
   233	    const parsed = parseYaml(frontmatter);
   234	    if (typeof parsed !== 'object' || parsed === null) {
   235	      return {} as GSDPreferences;
   236	    }
   237	    return parsed as GSDPreferences;
   238	  } catch (e) {
   239	    console.error("[parseFrontmatterBlock] YAML parse error:", e);
   240	    return {} as GSDPreferences;
   241	  }
   242	}
   243	
   244	/**
   245	 * Parse heading+list format into a nested object, then cast to GSDPreferences.
   246	 * Handles markdown like:
   247	 *   ## Git
   248	 *   - isolation: none
   249	 *   - commit_docs: true
   250	 *   ## Models
   251	 *   - planner: sonnet
   252	 */
   253	function parseHeadingListFormat(content: string): GSDPreferences {
   254	  const result: Record<string, Record<string, string>> = {};
   255	  let currentSection: string | null = null;
   256	
   257	  for (const rawLine of content.split('\n')) {
   258	    const line = rawLine.replace(/\r$/, '');
   259	    const headingMatch = line.match(/^##\s+(.+)$/);
   260	    if (headingMatch) {
   261	      currentSection = headingMatch[1].trim().toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '_');
   262	      continue;
   263	    }
   264	    if (currentSection) {
   265	      const itemMatch = line.match(/^-\s+([^:]+):\s*(.*)$/);
   266	      if (itemMatch) {
   267	        if (!result[currentSection]) result[currentSection] = {};
   268	        const value = itemMatch[2].trim();
   269	        // Coerce "true"/"false" strings and numbers
   270	        result[currentSection][itemMatch[1].trim()] = value;
   271	      }
   272	    }
   273	  }
   274	
   275	  // Convert string values to appropriate types via YAML parser for each section
   276	  const typed: Record<string, unknown> = {};
   277	  for (const [section, entries] of Object.entries(result)) {
   278	    const yamlLines = Object.entries(entries).map(([k, v]) => `${k}: ${v}`).join('\n');
   279	    try {
   280	      typed[section] = parseYaml(yamlLines);
   281	    } catch {
   282	      typed[section] = entries;
   283	    }
   284	  }
   285	
   286	  return typed as GSDPreferences;
   287	}
   288	
   289	// ─── Merging ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   290	
   291	/**
   292	 * Apply mode defaults as the lowest-priority layer.
   293	 * Mode defaults fill in undefined fields; any explicit user value wins.
   294	 */
   295	export function applyModeDefaults(mode: WorkflowMode, prefs: GSDPreferences): GSDPreferences {
   296	  const defaults = MODE_DEFAULTS[mode];
   297	  if (!defaults) return prefs;
   298	  return mergePreferences(defaults, prefs);
   299	}
   300	
   301	function mergePreferences(base: GSDPreferences, override: GSDPreferences): GSDPreferences {
   302	  return {
   303	    version: override.version ?? base.version,
   304	    mode: override.mode ?? base.mode,
   305	    always_use_skills: mergeStringLists(base.always_use_skills, override.always_use_skills),
   306	    prefer_skills: mergeStringLists(base.prefer_skills, override.prefer_skills),
   307	    avoid_skills: mergeStringLists(base.avoid_skills, override.avoid_skills),
   308	    skill_rules: [...(base.skill_rules ?? []), ...(override.skill_rules ?? [])],
   309	    custom_instructions: mergeStringLists(base.custom_instructions, override.custom_instructions),
   310	    models: { ...(base.models ?? {}), ...(override.models ?? {}) },
   311	    skill_discovery: override.skill_discovery ?? base.skill_discovery,
   312	    skill_staleness_days: override.skill_staleness_days ?? base.skill_staleness_days,
   313	    auto_supervisor: { ...(base.auto_supervisor ?? {}), ...(override.auto_supervisor ?? {}) },
   314	    uat_dispatch: override.uat_dispatch ?? base.uat_dispatch,
   315	    unique_milestone_ids: override.unique_milestone_ids ?? base.unique_milestone_ids,
   316	    budget_ceiling: override.budget_ceiling ?? base.budget_ceiling,
   317	    budget_enforcement: override.budget_enforcement ?? base.budget_enforcement,
   318	    context_pause_threshold: override.context_pause_threshold ?? base.context_pause_threshold,
   319	    notifications: (base.notifications || override.notifications)
   320	      ? { ...(base.notifications ?? {}), ...(override.notifications ?? {}) }
   321	      : undefined,
   322	    cmux: (base.cmux || override.cmux)
   323	      ? { ...(base.cmux ?? {}), ...(override.cmux ?? {}) }
   324	      : undefined,
   325	    remote_questions: override.remote_questions
   326	      ? { ...(base.remote_questions ?? {}), ...override.remote_questions }
   327	      : base.remote_questions,
   328	    git: (base.git || override.git)
   329	      ? { ...(base.git ?? {}), ...(override.git ?? {}) }
   330	      : undefined,
   331	    post_unit_hooks: mergePostUnitHooks(base.post_unit_hooks, override.post_unit_hooks),
   332	    pre_dispatch_hooks: mergePreDispatchHooks(base.pre_dispatch_hooks, override.pre_dispatch_hooks),
   333	    dynamic_routing: (base.dynamic_routing || override.dynamic_routing)
   334	      ? { ...(base.dynamic_routing ?? {}), ...(override.dynamic_routing ?? {}) } as DynamicRoutingConfig
   335	      : undefined,
   336	    token_profile: override.token_profile ?? base.token_profile,
   337	    phases: (base.phases || override.phases)
   338	      ? { ...(base.phases ?? {}), ...(override.phases ?? {}) }
   339	      : undefined,
   340	    parallel: (base.parallel || override.parallel)
   341	      ? { ...(base.parallel ?? {}), ...(override.parallel ?? {}) } as import("./types.js").ParallelConfig
   342	      : undefined,
   343	    verification_commands: mergeStringLists(base.verification_commands, override.verification_commands),
   344	    verification_auto_fix: override.verification_auto_fix ?? base.verification_auto_fix,
   345	    verification_max_retries: override.verification_max_retries ?? base.verification_max_retries,
   346	    search_provider: override.search_provider ?? base.search_provider,
   347	    context_selection: override.context_selection ?? base.context_selection,
   348	    auto_visualize: override.auto_visualize ?? base.auto_visualize,
   349	    auto_report: override.auto_report ?? base.auto_report,
   350	    github: (base.github || override.github)
   351	      ? { ...(base.github ?? {}), ...(override.github ?? {}) } as import("../github-sync/types.js").GitHubSyncConfig
   352	      : undefined,
   353	    service_tier: override.service_tier ?? base.service_tier,
   354	    forensics_dedup: override.forensics_dedup ?? base.forensics_dedup,
   355	    show_token_cost: override.show_token_cost ?? base.show_token_cost,
   356	    experimental: (base.experimental || override.experimental)
   357	      ? { ...(base.experimental ?? {}), ...(override.experimental ?? {}) }
   358	      : undefined,
   359	  };
   360	}
   361	
   362	function mergeStringLists(base?: unknown, override?: unknown): string[] | undefined {
   363	  const merged = [
   364	    ...normalizeStringArray(base),
   365	    ...normalizeStringArray(override),
   366	  ]
   367	    .map((item) => item.trim())
   368	    .filter(Boolean);
   369	  return merged.length > 0 ? Array.from(new Set(merged)) : undefined;
   370	}
   371	
   372	function mergePostUnitHooks(
   373	  base?: PostUnitHookConfig[],
   374	  override?: PostUnitHookConfig[],
   375	): PostUnitHookConfig[] | undefined {
   376	  if (!base?.length && !override?.length) return undefined;
   377	  const merged = [...(base ?? [])];
   378	  for (const hook of override ?? []) {
   379	    // Override hooks with same name replace base hooks
   380	    const idx = merged.findIndex(h => h.name === hook.name);
   381	    if (idx >= 0) {
   382	      merged[idx] = hook;
   383	    } else {
   384	      merged.push(hook);
   385	    }
   386	  }
   387	  return merged.length > 0 ? merged : undefined;
   388	}
   389	
   390	function mergePreDispatchHooks(
   391	  base?: PreDispatchHookConfig[],
   392	  override?: PreDispatchHookConfig[],
   393	): PreDispatchHookConfig[] | undefined {
   394	  if (!base?.length && !override?.length) return undefined;
   395	  const merged = [...(base ?? [])];
   396	  for (const hook of override ?? []) {
   397	    const idx = merged.findIndex(h => h.name === hook.name);
   398	    if (idx >= 0) {
   399	      merged[idx] = hook;
   400	    } else {
   401	      merged.push(hook);
   402	    }
   403	  }
   404	  return merged.length > 0 ? merged : undefined;
   405	}

   280	// ─── Core Detection ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   281	
   282	/**
   283	 * Detect the full project state for a given directory.
   284	 * This is the main entry point — calls all sub-detectors.
   285	 */
   286	export function detectProjectState(basePath: string): ProjectDetection {
   287	  const v1 = detectV1Planning(basePath);
   288	  const v2 = detectV2Gsd(basePath);
   289	  const projectSignals = detectProjectSignals(basePath);
   290	  const globalSetup = hasGlobalSetup();
   291	  const firstEver = isFirstEverLaunch();
   292	
   293	  let state: ProjectDetection["state"];
   294	  if (v2 && v2.milestoneCount > 0) {
   295	    state = "v2-gsd";
   296	  } else if (v2 && v2.milestoneCount === 0) {
   297	    state = "v2-gsd-empty";
   298	  } else if (v1) {
   299	    state = "v1-planning";
   300	  } else {
   301	    state = "none";
   302	  }
   303	
   304	  return {
   305	    state,
   306	    isFirstEverLaunch: firstEver,
   307	    hasGlobalSetup: globalSetup,
   308	    v1: v1 ?? undefined,
   309	    v2: v2 ?? undefined,
   310	    projectSignals,
   311	  };
   312	}
   313	
   314	// ─── V1 Planning Detection ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   315	
   316	/**
   317	 * Detect a v1 .planning/ directory with GSD v1 markers.
   318	 * Returns null if no .planning/ directory found.
   319	 */
   320	export function detectV1Planning(basePath: string): V1Detection | null {
   321	  const planningPath = join(basePath, ".planning");
   322	
   323	  if (!existsSync(planningPath)) return null;
   324	
   325	  try {
   326	    const stat = statSync(planningPath);
   327	    if (!stat.isDirectory()) return null;
   328	  } catch {
   329	    return null;
   330	  }
   331	
   332	  const hasRoadmap = existsSync(join(planningPath, "ROADMAP.md"));
   333	  const phasesPath = join(planningPath, "phases");
   334	  const hasPhasesDir = existsSync(phasesPath);
   335	
   336	  let phaseCount = 0;
   337	  if (hasPhasesDir) {
   338	    try {
   339	      const entries = readdirSync(phasesPath, { withFileTypes: true });
   340	      phaseCount = entries.filter(e => e.isDirectory()).length;
   341	    } catch {
   342	      // unreadable — report 0
   343	    }
   344	  }
   345	
   346	  return {
   347	    path: planningPath,
   348	    hasPhasesDir,
   349	    hasRoadmap,
   350	    phaseCount,
   351	  };
   352	}
   353	
   354	// ─── V2 GSD Detection ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   355	
   356	function detectV2Gsd(basePath: string): V2Detection | null {
   357	  const gsdPath = gsdRoot(basePath);
   358	
   359	  if (!existsSync(gsdPath)) return null;
   360	
   361	  const hasPreferences =
   362	    existsSync(join(gsdPath, "preferences.md")) ||
   363	    existsSync(join(gsdPath, "PREFERENCES.md"));
   364	
   365	  const hasContext = existsSync(join(gsdPath, "CONTEXT.md"));
   366	
   367	  let milestoneCount = 0;
   368	  const milestonesPath = join(gsdPath, "milestones");
   369	  if (existsSync(milestonesPath)) {
   370	    try {
   371	      const entries = readdirSync(milestonesPath, { withFileTypes: true });
   372	      milestoneCount = entries.filter(e => e.isDirectory()).length;
   373	    } catch {
   374	      // unreadable — report 0
   375	    }
   376	  }
   377	
   378	  return { milestoneCount, hasPreferences, hasContext };
   379	}
   380	
   381	// ─── Project Signals Detection ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   382	
   383	/**
   384	 * Quick filesystem scan for project ecosystem markers.
   385	 * Reads only file existence + minimal content (package.json for monorepo/scripts).
   386	 */
   387	export function detectProjectSignals(basePath: string): ProjectSignals {
   388	  const detectedFiles: string[] = [];
   389	  let primaryLanguage: string | undefined;
   390	
   391	  // Detect project files
   392	  for (const file of PROJECT_FILES) {
   393	    if (existsSync(join(basePath, file))) {
   394	      detectedFiles.push(file);
   395	      if (!primaryLanguage) {
   396	        primaryLanguage = LANGUAGE_MAP[file];
   397	      }
   398	    }
   399	  }
   400	
   401	  // Bounded recursive scan for nested markers and dependency files.
   402	  // This covers common brownfield layouts like src/App/App.csproj,
   403	  // db/migrations/*.sql, src/components/*.vue, and services/api/pyproject.toml
   404	  // without walking the entire repo or diving into heavyweight folders.
   405	  const scannedFiles = scanProjectFiles(basePath);
   406	
   407	  for (const file of PROJECT_FILES) {
   408	    if (detectedFiles.includes(file) || ROOT_ONLY_PROJECT_FILES.has(file)) continue;
   409	    const hasMatch = file === "requirements.txt"
   410	      ? scannedFiles.some(isPythonRequirementsFile)
   411	      : scannedFiles.some((scannedFile) => matchesProjectFileMarker(scannedFile, file));
   412	    if (hasMatch) {
   413	      pushUnique(detectedFiles, file);
   414	      if (!primaryLanguage && LANGUAGE_MAP[file]) {
   415	        primaryLanguage = LANGUAGE_MAP[file];
   416	      }
   417	    }
   418	  }
   419	
   420	  if (scannedFiles.some((file) => SQLITE_EXTENSIONS.some((ext) => file.endsWith(ext)))) {
   421	    pushUnique(detectedFiles, "*.sqlite");
   422	  }
   423	  if (scannedFiles.some((file) => SQL_EXTENSIONS.some((ext) => file.endsWith(ext)))) {
   424	    pushUnique(detectedFiles, "*.sql");
   425	  }
   426	
   427	  const hasCsproj = scannedFiles.some((file) => file.endsWith(".csproj"));
   428	  const hasFsproj = scannedFiles.some((file) => file.endsWith(".fsproj"));
   429	  const hasSln = scannedFiles.some((file) => file.endsWith(".sln"));
   430	
   431	  if (hasCsproj) {
   432	    pushUnique(detectedFiles, "*.csproj");
   433	    if (!primaryLanguage) primaryLanguage = "csharp";
   434	  }
   435	  if (hasFsproj) {
   436	    pushUnique(detectedFiles, "*.fsproj");
   437	    if (!primaryLanguage) primaryLanguage = "fsharp";
   438	  }
   439	  if (hasSln) {
   440	    pushUnique(detectedFiles, "*.sln");
   441	    if (!primaryLanguage) primaryLanguage = "dotnet";
   442	  }
   443	
   444	  if (scannedFiles.some((file) => VUE_EXTENSIONS.some((ext) => file.endsWith(ext)))) {
   445	    pushUnique(detectedFiles, "*.vue");
   446	  }
   447	
   448	  // Python framework detection — scan dependency files for framework-specific packages.
   449	  // Adds synthetic markers (e.g. "dep:fastapi") so skill catalog matchFiles can reference them.
   450	  const dependencyFiles = scannedFiles.filter((file) =>
   451	    isPythonRequirementsFile(file) || file.endsWith("pyproject.toml"),
   452	  );
   453	  if (containsFastapiDependency(basePath, dependencyFiles)) {
   454	    pushUnique(detectedFiles, "dep:fastapi");
   455	  }
   456	
   457	  const springBootBuildFiles = scannedFiles.filter((file) =>
   458	    file.endsWith("pom.xml") || file.endsWith("build.gradle") || file.endsWith("build.gradle.kts"),
   459	  );
   460	  const springBootVersionCatalogs = scannedFiles.filter((file) => file.endsWith(".versions.toml"));
   461	  const springBootSettingsFiles = scannedFiles.filter((file) =>
   462	    file.endsWith("settings.gradle") || file.endsWith("settings.gradle.kts"),
   463	  );
   464	  if (containsSpringBootMarker(basePath, springBootBuildFiles, springBootVersionCatalogs, springBootSettingsFiles)) {
   465	    pushUnique(detectedFiles, "dep:spring-boot");
   466	    if (!primaryLanguage) {
   467	      primaryLanguage = "java/kotlin";
   468	    }
   469	  }
   470	
   471	  // Git repo detection
   472	  const isGitRepo = existsSync(join(basePath, ".git"));
   473	
   474	  // Xcode platform detection — parse SDKROOT from project.pbxproj
   475	  const xcodePlatforms = detectXcodePlatforms(basePath);
   476	
   477	  // Set primaryLanguage to swift when an Xcode project is found but no
   478	  // Package.swift was detected (CocoaPods or SPM-less projects).
   479	  if (!primaryLanguage && xcodePlatforms.length > 0) {
   480	    primaryLanguage = "swift";
   481	  }
   482	
   483	  // Monorepo detection
   484	  let isMonorepo = false;
   485	  for (const marker of MONOREPO_MARKERS) {
   486	    if (existsSync(join(basePath, marker))) {
   487	      isMonorepo = true;
   488	      break;
   489	    }
   490	  }
   491	  // Also check package.json workspaces
   492	  if (!isMonorepo && detectedFiles.includes("package.json")) {
   493	    isMonorepo = packageJsonHasWorkspaces(basePath);
   494	  }
   495	
   496	  // CI detection
   497	  let hasCI = false;
   498	  for (const marker of CI_MARKERS) {
   499	    if (existsSync(join(basePath, marker))) {
   500	      hasCI = true;
   501	      break;
   502	    }
   503	  }
   504	
   505	  // Test detection
   506	  let hasTests = false;
   507	  for (const marker of TEST_MARKERS) {
   508	    if (existsSync(join(basePath, marker))) {
   509	      hasTests = true;
   510	      break;
   511	    }
   512	  }
   513	
   514	  // Package manager detection
   515	  const packageManager = detectPackageManager(basePath);
   516	
   517	  // Verification commands
   518	  const verificationCommands = detectVerificationCommands(basePath, detectedFiles, packageManager);
   519	
   520	  return {
   521	    detectedFiles,
   522	    isGitRepo,
   523	    isMonorepo,
   524	    primaryLanguage,
   525	    xcodePlatforms,
   526	    hasCI,
   527	    hasTests,
   528	    packageManager,
   529	    verificationCommands,
   530	  };
   531	}
   532	
   533	// ─── Xcode Platform Detection ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
   534	
   535	/** Known SDKROOT values → canonical platform names. */
   536	const SDKROOT_MAP: Record<string, XcodePlatform> = {
   537	  iphoneos: "iphoneos",
   538	  iphonesimulator: "iphoneos",      // simulator builds still target iOS
   539	  macosx: "macosx",
   540	  watchos: "watchos",
   541	  watchsimulator: "watchos",
   542	  appletvos: "appletvos",
   543	  appletvsimulator: "appletvos",
   544	  xros: "xros",
   545	  xrsimulator: "xros",
   546	};
   547	
   548	/** Regex for SUPPORTED_PLATFORMS — fallback when SDKROOT = auto (Xcode 15+). */
   549	const SUPPORTED_PLATFORMS_RE = /SUPPORTED_PLATFORMS\s*=\s*"([^"]+)"/gi;
   550	
   551	/** Read at most `maxBytes` from a file without loading the full file into memory. */
   552	function readBounded(filePath: string, maxBytes: number): string {
   553	  const buf = Buffer.alloc(maxBytes);
   554	  const fd = openSync(filePath, "r");
   555	  try {
   556	    const bytesRead = readSync(fd, buf, 0, maxBytes, 0);
   557	    return buf.toString("utf-8", 0, bytesRead);
   558	  } finally {
   559	    closeSync(fd);
   560	  }
   561	}
   562	
   563	/** Common subdirectories where .xcodeproj may live in monorepos / standard layouts. */
   564	const XCODE_SUBDIRS = ["ios", "macos", "app", "apps"] as const;

   248	/**
   249	 * Show migration offer when .planning/ is detected.
   250	 * Returns 'migrate', 'fresh', or 'cancel'.
   251	 */
   252	export async function offerMigration(
   253	  ctx: ExtensionCommandContext,
   254	  v1: NonNullable<ProjectDetection["v1"]>,
   255	): Promise<"migrate" | "fresh" | "cancel"> {
   256	  const summary = [

   258	  ];

   261	  }

   263	    summary.push("Has ROADMAP.md");
   264	  }
   265	
   266	  const choice = await showNextAction(ctx, {
   267	    title: "GSD — Legacy Project Detected",
   268	    summary,
   269	    actions: [
   270	      {
   271	        id: "migrate",
   272	        label: "Migrate to GSD v2",
   273	        description: "Convert .planning/ to .gsd/ format",
   274	        recommended: true,
   275	      },
   276	      {
   277	        id: "fresh",
   278	        label: "Start fresh",
   279	        description: "Ignore .planning/ and create new .gsd/",
   280	      },
   281	    ],
   282	    notYetMessage: "Run /gsd init when ready.",
   283	  });
   284	
   285	  if (choice === "not_yet") return "cancel";
   286	  return choice as "migrate" | "fresh";
   287	}

   289	// ─── Re-init Handler ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   290	
   291	/**
   292	 * Handle /gsd init when .gsd/ already exists.
   293	 * Offers preference reset without destructive milestone deletion.
   294	 */
   295	export async function handleReinit(
   296	  ctx: ExtensionCommandContext,
   297	  detection: ProjectDetection,
   298	): Promise<void> {
   299	  const summary = ["GSD is already initialized in this project."];
   300	  if (detection.v2) {
   301	    summary.push(`${detection.v2.milestoneCount} milestone(s) found`);
   302	    summary.push(`Preferences: ${detection.v2.hasPreferences ? "configured" : "not set"}`);
   303	  }
   304	
   305	  const choice = await showNextAction(ctx, {
   306	    title: "GSD — Already Initialized",
   307	    summary,
   308	    actions: [
   309	      {
   310	        id: "prefs",
   311	        label: "Re-configure preferences",
   312	        description: "Update project preferences without affecting milestones",
   313	        recommended: true,
   314	      },
   315	      {
   316	        id: "cancel",
   317	        label: "Cancel",
   318	        description: "Keep everything as-is",
   319	      },
   320	    ],
   321	    notYetMessage: "Run /gsd init when ready.",
   322	  });
   323	
   324	  if (choice === "prefs") {

   326	  }

   329	// ─── Git Preferences Customization ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   330	
   331	async function customizeGitPrefs(
   332	  ctx: ExtensionCommandContext,
   333	  prefs: ProjectPreferences,
   334	  signals: ProjectSignals,
   335	): Promise<void> {
   336	  // Isolation strategy
   337	  const hasSubmodules = existsSync(join(process.cwd(), ".gitmodules"));
   338	  const isolationActions = [
   339	    { id: "worktree", label: "Worktree", description: "Isolated git worktree per milestone (recommended)", recommended: !hasSubmodules },
   340	    { id: "branch", label: "Branch", description: "Work on branches in project root (better for submodules)", recommended: hasSubmodules },
   341	    { id: "none", label: "None", description: "No isolation — commits on current branch" },
   342	  ];
   343	
   344	  const isolationSummary = hasSubmodules
   345	    ? ["Submodules detected — branch mode recommended over worktree."]
   346	    : ["Worktree isolation creates a separate copy for each milestone."];
   347	
   348	  const isolationChoice = await showNextAction(ctx, {
   349	    title: "Git isolation strategy",
   350	    summary: isolationSummary,
   351	    actions: isolationActions,
   352	  });
   353	  if (isolationChoice !== "not_yet") {
   354	    prefs.gitIsolation = isolationChoice as "worktree" | "branch" | "none";
   355	  }
   356	}
   357	
   358	// ─── Advanced Preferences Customization ─────────────────────────────────────────
   359	
   360	async function customizeAdvancedPrefs(
   361	  ctx: ExtensionCommandContext,
   362	  prefs: ProjectPreferences,
   363	): Promise<void> {
   364	  // Token profile
   365	  const profileChoice = await showNextAction(ctx, {
   366	    title: "Token usage profile",
   367	    summary: [
   368	      "Controls how much context GSD uses per task.",
   369	      "Budget: cheaper, faster. Quality: thorough, more expensive.",
   370	    ],
   371	    actions: [
   372	      { id: "balanced", label: "Balanced", description: "Good trade-off (default)", recommended: true },
   373	      { id: "budget", label: "Budget", description: "Minimize token usage" },
   374	      { id: "quality", label: "Quality", description: "Maximize thoroughness" },
   375	    ],
   376	  });
   377	  if (profileChoice !== "not_yet") {
   378	    prefs.tokenProfile = profileChoice as "budget" | "balanced" | "quality";
   379	  }
   380	
   381	  // Skip research
   382	  const researchChoice = await showNextAction(ctx, {
   383	    title: "Research phase",
   384	    summary: [
   385	      "GSD can research the codebase before planning each milestone.",
   386	      "Small projects may not need this step.",
   387	    ],
   388	    actions: [
   389	      { id: "keep", label: "Keep research", description: "Explore codebase before planning", recommended: true },
   390	      { id: "skip", label: "Skip research", description: "Go straight to planning" },
   391	    ],
   392	  });
   393	  prefs.skipResearch = researchChoice === "skip";
   394	
   395	  // Auto-push
   396	  const pushChoice = await showNextAction(ctx, {
   397	    title: "Auto-push after merge",
   398	    summary: [
   399	      "After merging a milestone branch, auto-push to remote?",
   400	      prefs.mode === "team"
   401	        ? "Team mode: usually disabled so changes go through PR review."
   402	        : "Solo mode: usually enabled for convenience.",
   403	    ],
   404	    actions: [
   405	      { id: "yes", label: "Yes", description: "Push automatically", recommended: prefs.mode === "solo" },
   406	      { id: "no", label: "No", description: "Manual push only", recommended: prefs.mode === "team" },
   407	    ],
   408	  });
   409	  prefs.autoPush = pushChoice !== "no";
   410	}

   412	// ─── Bootstrap ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   413	
   414	function bootstrapGsdDirectory(
   415	  basePath: string,
   416	  prefs: ProjectPreferences,
   417	  signals: ProjectSignals,
   418	): void {
   419	  // Final safety check before writing any files
   420	  assertSafeDirectory(basePath);
   421	
   422	  const gsd = gsdRoot(basePath);
   423	  mkdirSync(join(gsd, "milestones"), { recursive: true });
   424	
   425	  // Write preferences.md from wizard answers
   426	  const preferencesContent = buildPreferencesFile(prefs);
   427	  writeFileSync(join(gsd, "preferences.md"), preferencesContent, "utf-8");
   428	
   429	  // Seed CONTEXT.md with detected project signals
   430	  const contextContent = buildContextSeed(signals);
   431	  if (contextContent) {
   432	    writeFileSync(join(gsd, "CONTEXT.md"), contextContent, "utf-8");
   433	  }
   434	}

    25	/** Extract body content after frontmatter closing delimiter, or null if none. */
    26	function extractBodyAfterFrontmatter(content: string): string | null {
    27	  const closingIdx = content.indexOf("\n---", content.indexOf("---"));
    28	  if (closingIdx === -1) return null;
    29	  const afterFrontmatter = content.slice(closingIdx + 4);
    30	  return afterFrontmatter.trim() ? afterFrontmatter : null;
    31	}

    33	// ─── Numeric validation helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    34	
    35	/** Parse a string as a non-negative integer, or return null on failure. */
    36	function tryParseInteger(val: string): number | null {
    37	  return /^\d+$/.test(val) ? Number(val) : null;
    38	}
    39	
    40	/** Parse a string as a finite number, or return null on failure. */
    41	function tryParseNumber(val: string): number | null {
    42	  const n = Number(val);
    43	  return !isNaN(n) && isFinite(n) ? n : null;
    44	}
    45	
    46	/** Parse a string as a number in the 0–100 range, or return null on failure. */
    47	function tryParsePercentage(val: string): number | null {
    48	  const n = Number(val);
    49	  return !isNaN(n) && n >= 0 && n <= 100 ? n : null;
    50	}

    52	export async function handlePrefs(args: string, ctx: ExtensionCommandContext): Promise<void> {
    53	  const trimmed = args.trim();
    54	
    55	  if (trimmed === "" || trimmed === "global" || trimmed === "wizard" || trimmed === "setup"
    56	    || trimmed === "wizard global" || trimmed === "setup global") {
    57	    await ensurePreferencesFile(getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath(), ctx, "global");
    58	    await handlePrefsWizard(ctx, "global");
    59	    return;
    60	  }
    61	
    62	  if (trimmed === "project" || trimmed === "wizard project" || trimmed === "setup project") {
    63	    await ensurePreferencesFile(getProjectGSDPreferencesPath(), ctx, "project");
    64	    await handlePrefsWizard(ctx, "project");
    65	    return;
    66	  }
    67	
    68	  if (trimmed === "import-claude" || trimmed === "import-claude global") {
    69	    await handleImportClaude(ctx, "global");
    70	    return;
    71	  }
    72	
    73	  if (trimmed === "import-claude project") {
    74	    await handleImportClaude(ctx, "project");
    75	    return;
    76	  }
    77	  if (trimmed === "status") {
    78	    const globalPrefs = loadGlobalGSDPreferences();
    79	    const projectPrefs = loadProjectGSDPreferences();
    80	    const canonicalGlobal = getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
    81	    const legacyGlobal = getLegacyGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
    82	    const globalStatus = globalPrefs
    83	      ? `present: ${globalPrefs.path}${globalPrefs.path === legacyGlobal ? " (legacy fallback)" : ""}`
    84	      : `missing: ${canonicalGlobal}`;
    85	    const projectStatus = projectPrefs ? `present: ${projectPrefs.path}` : `missing: ${getProjectGSDPreferencesPath()}`;
    86	
    87	    const lines = [`GSD skill prefs — global ${globalStatus}; project ${projectStatus}`];
    88	
    89	    const effective = loadEffectiveGSDPreferences();
    90	    let hasUnresolved = false;
    91	    if (effective) {
    92	      const report = resolveAllSkillReferences(effective.preferences, process.cwd());
    93	      const resolved = [...report.resolutions.values()].filter(r => r.method !== "unresolved");
    94	      hasUnresolved = report.warnings.length > 0;
    95	      if (resolved.length > 0 || hasUnresolved) {
    96	        lines.push(`Skills: ${resolved.length} resolved, ${report.warnings.length} unresolved`);
    97	      }
    98	      if (hasUnresolved) {
    99	        lines.push(`Unresolved: ${report.warnings.join(", ")}`);
   100	      }
   101	    }
   102	
   103	    ctx.ui.notify(lines.join("\n"), hasUnresolved ? "warning" : "info");
   104	    return;
   105	  }
   106	
   107	  ctx.ui.notify("Usage: /gsd prefs [global|project|status|wizard|setup|import-claude [global|project]]", "info");
   108	}
   109	
   110	export async function handleImportClaude(ctx: ExtensionCommandContext, scope: "global" | "project"): Promise<void> {
   111	  const path = scope === "project" ? getProjectGSDPreferencesPath() : getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
   112	  if (!existsSync(path)) {
   113	    await ensurePreferencesFile(path, ctx, scope);
   114	  }
   115	
   116	  const readPrefs = (): Record<string, unknown> => {
   117	    if (!existsSync(path)) return { version: 1 };
   118	    const content = readFileSync(path, "utf-8");
   119	    const [frontmatterLines] = splitFrontmatter(content);
   120	    return frontmatterLines ? parseFrontmatterMap(frontmatterLines) : { version: 1 };
   121	  };
   122	
   123	  const writePrefs = async (prefs: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void> => {
   124	    prefs.version = prefs.version || 1;
   125	    const frontmatter = serializePreferencesToFrontmatter(prefs);
   126	    let body = "\n# GSD Skill Preferences\n\nSee `~/.gsd/agent/extensions/gsd/docs/preferences-reference.md` for full field documentation and examples.\n";
   127	    if (existsSync(path)) {
   128	      const preserved = extractBodyAfterFrontmatter(readFileSync(path, "utf-8"));
   129	      if (preserved) body = preserved;
   130	    }
   131	    await saveFile(path, `---\n${frontmatter}---${body}`);
   132	  };
   133	
   134	  await runClaudeImportFlow(ctx, scope, readPrefs, writePrefs);
   135	}
   136	
   137	export async function handlePrefsMode(ctx: ExtensionCommandContext, scope: "global" | "project"): Promise<void> {
   138	  const path = scope === "project" ? getProjectGSDPreferencesPath() : getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
   139	  const existing = scope === "project" ? loadProjectGSDPreferences() : loadGlobalGSDPreferences();
   140	  const prefs: Record<string, unknown> = existing?.preferences ? { ...existing.preferences } : {};
   141	
   142	  await configureMode(ctx, prefs);
   143	
   144	  // Serialize and save
   145	  prefs.version = prefs.version || 1;
   146	  const frontmatter = serializePreferencesToFrontmatter(prefs);
   147	
   148	  let body = "\n# GSD Skill Preferences\n\nSee `~/.gsd/agent/extensions/gsd/docs/preferences-reference.md` for full field documentation and examples.\n";
   149	  if (existsSync(path)) {
   150	    const preserved = extractBodyAfterFrontmatter(readFileSync(path, "utf-8"));
   151	    if (preserved) body = preserved;
   152	  }
   153	
   154	  const content = `---\n${frontmatter}---${body}`;
   155	  await saveFile(path, content);
   156	  await ctx.waitForIdle();
   157	  await ctx.reload();
   158	  ctx.ui.notify(`Saved ${scope} preferences to ${path}`, "info");
   159	}

   161	/** Build short summary strings for each preference category. */
   162	export function buildCategorySummaries(prefs: Record<string, unknown>): Record<string, string> {
   163	  // Mode
   164	  const mode = prefs.mode as string | undefined;
   165	  const modeSummary = mode ?? "(not set)";
   166	
   167	  // Models
   168	  const models = prefs.models as Record<string, string> | undefined;
   169	  let modelsSummary = "(not configured)";
   170	  if (models && Object.keys(models).length > 0) {
   171	    const parts = Object.entries(models).map(([phase, model]) => `${phase}: ${model}`);
   172	    modelsSummary = parts.join(", ");
   173	  }
   174	
   175	  // Timeouts
   176	  const autoSup = prefs.auto_supervisor as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
   177	  let timeoutsSummary = "(defaults)";
   178	  if (autoSup && Object.keys(autoSup).length > 0) {
   179	    const soft = autoSup.soft_timeout_minutes ?? "20";
   180	    const idle = autoSup.idle_timeout_minutes ?? "10";
   181	    const hard = autoSup.hard_timeout_minutes ?? "30";
   182	    timeoutsSummary = `soft: ${soft}m, idle: ${idle}m, hard: ${hard}m`;
   183	  }
   184	
   185	  // Git
   186	  const git = prefs.git as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
   187	  let gitSummary = "(defaults)";
   188	  if (git && Object.keys(git).length > 0) {
   189	    const branch = git.main_branch ?? "main";
   190	    const push = git.auto_push ? "on" : "off";
   191	    gitSummary = `main: ${branch}, push: ${push}`;
   192	  }
   193	
   194	  // Skills
   195	  const discovery = prefs.skill_discovery as string | undefined;
   196	  const uat = prefs.uat_dispatch;
   197	  let skillsSummary = "(not configured)";
   198	  if (discovery || uat !== undefined) {
   199	    const parts: string[] = [];
   200	    if (discovery) parts.push(`discovery: ${discovery}`);
   201	    if (uat !== undefined) parts.push(`uat: ${uat}`);
   202	    skillsSummary = parts.join(", ");
   203	  }
   204	
   205	  // Budget
   206	  const ceiling = prefs.budget_ceiling;
   207	  const enforcement = prefs.budget_enforcement as string | undefined;
   208	  let budgetSummary = "(no limit)";
   209	  if (ceiling !== undefined) {
   210	    budgetSummary = `$${ceiling}`;
   211	    if (enforcement) budgetSummary += ` / ${enforcement}`;
   212	  } else if (enforcement) {
   213	    budgetSummary = enforcement;
   214	  }
   215	
   216	  // Notifications
   217	  const notif = prefs.notifications as Record<string, boolean> | undefined;
   218	  let notifSummary = "(defaults)";
   219	  if (notif && Object.keys(notif).length > 0) {
   220	    const allKeys = ["enabled", "on_complete", "on_error", "on_budget", "on_milestone", "on_attention"];
   221	    const enabledCount = allKeys.filter(k => notif[k] !== false).length;
   222	    notifSummary = `${enabledCount}/${allKeys.length} enabled`;
   223	  }
   224	
   225	  // Advanced
   226	  const uniqueIds = prefs.unique_milestone_ids;
   227	  let advancedSummary = "(defaults)";
   228	  if (uniqueIds !== undefined) {
   229	    advancedSummary = `unique IDs: ${uniqueIds ? "on" : "off"}`;
   230	  }
   231	
   232	  return {
   233	    mode: modeSummary,
   234	    models: modelsSummary,
   235	    timeouts: timeoutsSummary,
   236	    git: gitSummary,
   237	    skills: skillsSummary,
   238	    budget: budgetSummary,
   239	    notifications: notifSummary,
   240	    advanced: advancedSummary,
   241	  };
   242	}

   244	// ─── Category configuration functions ────────────────────────────────────────
   245	
   246	async function configureModels(ctx: ExtensionCommandContext, prefs: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void> {
   247	  const modelPhases = ["research", "planning", "execution", "completion"] as const;
   248	  const models: Record<string, string> = (prefs.models as Record<string, string>) ?? {};
   249	
   250	  const availableModels = ctx.modelRegistry.getAvailable();
   251	  if (availableModels.length > 0) {
   252	    // Group models by provider, sorted alphabetically
   253	    const byProvider = new Map<string, typeof availableModels>();
   254	    for (const m of availableModels) {
   255	      let group = byProvider.get(m.provider);
   256	      if (!group) {
   257	        group = [];
   258	        byProvider.set(m.provider, group);
   259	      }
   260	      group.push(m);
   261	    }
   262	    const providers = Array.from(byProvider.keys()).sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b));
   263	    // Sort models within each provider
   264	    for (const group of byProvider.values()) {
   265	      group.sort((a, b) => a.id.localeCompare(b.id));
   266	    }
   267	
   268	    // Build provider menu with model counts
   269	    const providerOptions = providers.map(p => {
   270	      const count = byProvider.get(p)!.length;
   271	      return `${p} (${count} models)`;
   272	    });
   273	    providerOptions.push("(keep current)", "(clear)", "(type manually)");
   274	
   275	    for (const phase of modelPhases) {
   276	      const current = models[phase] ?? "";
   277	      const phaseLabel = `Model for ${phase} phase${current ? ` (current: ${current})` : ""}`;
   278	
   279	      // Step 1: pick provider
   280	      const providerChoice = await ctx.ui.select(`${phaseLabel} — choose provider:`, providerOptions);
   281	      if (!providerChoice || typeof providerChoice !== "string" || providerChoice === "(keep current)") continue;
   282	
   283	      if (providerChoice === "(clear)") {
   284	        delete models[phase];
   285	        continue;
   286	      }
   287	
   288	      if (providerChoice === "(type manually)") {
   289	        const input = await ctx.ui.input(
   290	          `${phaseLabel} — enter model ID:`,
   291	          current || "e.g. claude-sonnet-4-20250514",
   292	        );
   293	        if (input !== null && input !== undefined) {
   294	          const val = input.trim();
   295	          if (val) models[phase] = val;
   296	        }
   297	        continue;
   298	      }
   299	
   300	      // Step 2: pick model within provider
   301	      const providerName = providerChoice.replace(/ \(\d+ models?\)$/, "");
   302	      const group = byProvider.get(providerName);
   303	      if (!group) continue;
   304	
   305	      const modelOptions = group.map(m => m.id);
   306	      modelOptions.push("(keep current)", "(clear)");
   307	
   308	      const modelChoice = await ctx.ui.select(`${phaseLabel} — ${providerName}:`, modelOptions);
   309	      if (modelChoice && typeof modelChoice === "string" && modelChoice !== "(keep current)") {
   310	        if (modelChoice === "(clear)") {
   311	          delete models[phase];
   312	        } else {
   313	          models[phase] = modelChoice;
   314	        }
   315	      }
   316	    }
   317	  } else {
   318	    for (const phase of modelPhases) {
   319	      const current = models[phase] ?? "";
   320	      const input = await ctx.ui.input(
   321	        `Model for ${phase} phase${current ? ` (current: ${current})` : ""}:`,
   322	        current || "e.g. claude-sonnet-4-20250514",
   323	      );
   324	      if (input !== null && input !== undefined) {
   325	        const val = input.trim();
   326	        if (val) {
   327	          models[phase] = val;
   328	        } else if (current) {
   329	          delete models[phase];
   330	        }
   331	      }
   332	    }
   333	  }
   334	  if (Object.keys(models).length > 0) {
   335	    prefs.models = models;
   336	  }
   337	}
   338	
   339	async function configureTimeouts(ctx: ExtensionCommandContext, prefs: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void> {
   340	  const autoSup: Record<string, unknown> = (prefs.auto_supervisor as Record<string, unknown>) ?? {};
   341	  const timeoutFields = [
   342	    { key: "soft_timeout_minutes", label: "Soft timeout (minutes)", defaultVal: "20" },
   343	    { key: "idle_timeout_minutes", label: "Idle timeout (minutes)", defaultVal: "10" },
   344	    { key: "hard_timeout_minutes", label: "Hard timeout (minutes)", defaultVal: "30" },
   345	  ] as const;
   346	
   347	  for (const field of timeoutFields) {
   348	    const current = autoSup[field.key];
   349	    const currentStr = current !== undefined && current !== null ? String(current) : "";
   350	    const input = await ctx.ui.input(
   351	      `${field.label}${currentStr ? ` (current: ${currentStr})` : ` (default: ${field.defaultVal})`}:`,
   352	      currentStr || field.defaultVal,
   353	    );
   354	    if (input !== null && input !== undefined) {
   355	      const val = input.trim();
   356	      const parsed = tryParseInteger(val);
   357	      if (val && parsed !== null) {
   358	        autoSup[field.key] = parsed;
   359	      } else if (val) {
   360	        ctx.ui.notify(`Invalid value "${val}" for ${field.label} — must be a whole number. Keeping previous value.`, "warning");
   361	      } else if (!val && currentStr) {
   362	        delete autoSup[field.key];
   363	      }
   364	    }
   365	  }

    87	/**
    88	 * Check whether `.gsd/` contains files tracked by git.
    89	 * If so, the project intentionally keeps `.gsd/` in version control
    90	 * and we must NOT add `.gsd` to `.gitignore` or attempt migration.
    91	 *
    92	 * Returns true if git tracks at least one file under `.gsd/`.
    93	 * Returns false (safe to ignore) if:
    94	 *   - Not a git repo
    95	 *   - `.gsd/` is a symlink (external state, should be ignored)
    96	 *   - `.gsd/` doesn't exist
    97	 *   - No tracked files found under `.gsd/`
    98	 */
    99	export function hasGitTrackedGsdFiles(basePath: string): boolean {
   100	  const localGsd = join(basePath, ".gsd");
   101	
   102	  // If .gsd doesn't exist or is already a symlink, no tracked files concern
   103	  if (!existsSync(localGsd)) return false;
   104	  try {
   105	    if (lstatSync(localGsd).isSymbolicLink()) return false;
   106	  } catch {
   107	    return false;
   108	  }
   109	
   110	  // Check if git tracks any files under .gsd/
   111	  try {
   112	    const tracked = nativeLsFiles(basePath, ".gsd");
   113	    if (tracked.length > 0) return true;
   114	
   115	    // nativeLsFiles swallows git failures and returns []. An empty result
   116	    // could mean "nothing tracked" OR "git failed silently". Verify git is
   117	    // reachable before trusting the empty result — if it isn't, fail safe
   118	    // by assuming files ARE tracked to prevent data loss.
   119	    execFileSync("git", ["rev-parse", "--git-dir"], {
   120	      cwd: basePath,
   121	      stdio: "pipe",
   122	      env: GIT_NO_PROMPT_ENV,
   123	    });
   124	
   125	    return false;
   126	  } catch {
   127	    // git unavailable, index locked, or repo corrupt — fail safe
   128	    return true;
   129	  }
   130	}
   131	
   132	/**
   133	 * Ensure basePath/.gitignore contains baseline ignore patterns.
   134	 * Creates the file if missing; appends missing patterns.
   135	 * Returns true if the file was created or modified, false if already complete.
   136	 *
   137	 * **Safety check:** If `.gsd/` contains git-tracked files (i.e., the project
   138	 * intentionally keeps `.gsd/` in version control), the `.gsd` ignore pattern
   139	 * is excluded to prevent data loss. Only the `.gsd` pattern is affected —
   140	 * all other baseline patterns are still applied normally.
   141	 */
   142	export function ensureGitignore(
   143	  basePath: string,
   144	  options?: { manageGitignore?: boolean },
   145	): boolean {
   146	  // If manage_gitignore is explicitly false, do not touch .gitignore at all
   147	  if (options?.manageGitignore === false) return false;
   148	
   149	  const gitignorePath = join(basePath, ".gitignore");
   150	
   151	  let existing = "";
   152	  if (existsSync(gitignorePath)) {
   153	    existing = readFileSync(gitignorePath, "utf-8");
   154	  }
   155	
   156	  // Parse existing lines (trimmed, ignoring comments and blanks)
   157	  const existingLines = new Set(
   158	    existing
   159	      .split("\n")
   160	      .map((l) => l.trim())
   161	      .filter((l) => l && !l.startsWith("#")),
   162	  );
   163	
   164	  // Determine which patterns to apply. If .gsd/ has tracked files,
   165	  // exclude the ".gsd" pattern to prevent deleting tracked state.
   166	  const gsdIsTracked = hasGitTrackedGsdFiles(basePath);
   167	  const patternsToApply = gsdIsTracked
   168	    ? BASELINE_PATTERNS.filter((p) => p !== ".gsd")
   169	    : BASELINE_PATTERNS;
   170	
   171	  // Find patterns not yet present
   172	  const missing = patternsToApply.filter((p) => !existingLines.has(p));
   173	
   174	  if (missing.length === 0) return false;
   175	
   176	  // Build the block to append
   177	  const block = [
   178	    "",
   179	    "# ── GSD baseline (auto-generated) ──",
   180	    ...missing,
   181	    "",
   182	  ].join("\n");
   183	
   184	  // Ensure existing content ends with a newline before appending
   185	  const prefix = existing && !existing.endsWith("\n") ? "\n" : "";
   186	  writeFileSync(gitignorePath, existing + prefix + block, "utf-8");
   187	
   188	  return true;
   189	}
   190	
   191	/**
   192	 * Remove BASELINE_PATTERNS runtime paths from the git index if they are
   193	 * currently tracked. This fixes repos that started tracking these files
   194	 * before the .gitignore rule was added — git continues tracking files
   195	 * already in the index even after .gitignore is updated.
   196	 *
   197	 * Only removes from the index (`--cached`), never from disk. Idempotent.
   198	 *
   199	 * Note: These are strictly runtime/ephemeral paths (activity logs, lock files,
   200	 * metrics, STATE.md). They are always safe to untrack, even when the project
   201	 * intentionally keeps other `.gsd/` files (like PROJECT.md, milestones/) in
   202	 * version control.
   203	 */
   204	export function untrackRuntimeFiles(basePath: string): void {
   205	  const runtimePaths = GSD_RUNTIME_PATTERNS;
   206	
   207	  for (const pattern of runtimePaths) {
   208	    // Use -r for directory patterns (trailing slash), strip the slash for the command
   209	    const target = pattern.endsWith("/") ? pattern.slice(0, -1) : pattern;
   210	    try {
   211	      nativeRmCached(basePath, [target]);
   212	    } catch {
   213	      // File not tracked or doesn't exist — expected, ignore
   214	    }
   215	  }
   216	}
   217	
   218	/**
   219	 * Ensure basePath/.gsd/preferences.md exists as an empty template.
   220	 * Creates the file with frontmatter only if it doesn't exist.
   221	 * Returns true if created, false if already exists.
   222	 *
   223	 * Checks both lowercase (canonical) and uppercase (legacy) to avoid
   224	 * creating a duplicate when an uppercase file already exists.
   225	 */
   226	export function ensurePreferences(basePath: string): boolean {
   227	  const preferencesPath = join(gsdRoot(basePath), "preferences.md");
   228	  const legacyPath = join(gsdRoot(basePath), "PREFERENCES.md");
   229	
   230	  if (existsSync(preferencesPath) || existsSync(legacyPath)) {
   231	    return false;
   232	  }
   233	
   234	  const template = `---
   235	version: 1
   236	always_use_skills: []
   237	prefer_skills: []
   238	avoid_skills: []
   239	skill_rules: []
   240	custom_instructions: []
   241	models: {}
   242	skill_discovery: {}
   243	auto_supervisor: {}
   244	---
   245	
   246	# GSD Skill Preferences
   247	
   248	Project-specific guidance for skill selection and execution preferences.
   249	
   250	See \`~/.gsd/agent/extensions/gsd/docs/preferences-reference.md\` for full field documentation and examples.
   251	
   252	## Fields
   253	
   254	- \`always_use_skills\`: Skills that must be available during all GSD operations
   255	- \`prefer_skills\`: Skills to prioritize when multiple options exist
   256	- \`avoid_skills\`: Skills to minimize or avoid (with lower priority than prefer)
   257	- \`skill_rules\`: Context-specific rules (e.g., "use tool X for Y type of work")
   258	- \`custom_instructions\`: Append-only project guidance (do not override system rules)
   259	- \`models\`: Model preferences for specific task types
   260	- \`skill_discovery\`: Automatic skill detection preferences
   261	- \`auto_supervisor\`: Supervision and gating rules for autonomous modes
   262	- \`git\`: Git preferences — \`main_branch\` (default branch name for new repos, e.g., "main", "master", "trunk"), \`auto_push\`, \`snapshots\`, etc.
   263	
   264	## Examples
   265	
   266	\`\`\`yaml
   267	prefer_skills:
   268	  - playwright
   269	  - resolve_library
   270	avoid_skills:
   271	  - subagent  # prefer direct execution in this project
   272	
   273	custom_instructions:
   274	  - "Always verify with browser_assert before marking UI work done"
   275	  - "Use Context7 for all library/framework decisions"
   276	\`\`\`
   277	`;
   278	
   279	  writeFileSync(preferencesPath, template, "utf-8");
   280	  return true;
   281	}
   282

    17	// via jiti at runtime. Importing it as .js fails because no .js exists
    18	// in dist/. See #592, #1110.

    21	export function saveRemoteQuestionsConfig(channel: "slack" | "discord" | "telegram", channelId: string): void {
    22	  const prefsPath = GLOBAL_PREFERENCES_PATH;
    23	  const block = [
    24	    "remote_questions:",
    25	    `  channel: ${channel}`,
    26	    `  channel_id: "${channelId}"`,
    27	    "  timeout_minutes: 5",
    28	    "  poll_interval_seconds: 5",
    29	  ].join("\n");
    30

    32	  const fmMatch = content.match(/^---\n([\s\S]*?)\n---/);
    33	  let next = content;
    34	
    35	  if (fmMatch) {
    36	    let frontmatter = fmMatch[1];
    37	    const regex = /remote_questions:[\s\S]*?(?=\n[a-zA-Z_]|\n---|$)/;
    38	    frontmatter = regex.test(frontmatter) ? frontmatter.replace(regex, block) : `${frontmatter.trimEnd()}\n${block}`;

    40	  } else {
    41	    next = `---\n${block}\n---\n\n${content}`;
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  mkdirSync(dirname(prefsPath), { recursive: true });
    45	  writeFileSync(prefsPath, next, "utf-8");

    47	function readAuthData(): Record<string, unknown> {
    48	  const authPath = getAuthPath()
    49	  if (!existsSync(authPath)) return {}
    50	  try {
    51	    const content = readFileSync(authPath, "utf-8")
    52	    const parsed = JSON.parse(content)
    53	    return typeof parsed === "object" && parsed !== null ? parsed as Record<string, unknown> : {}
    54	  } catch { return {} }
    55	}

    57	function writeAuthData(data: Record<string, unknown>): void {
    58	  const authPath = getAuthPath()
    59	  const parentDir = dirname(authPath)
    60	  if (!existsSync(parentDir)) mkdirSync(parentDir, { recursive: true, mode: 0o700 })
    61	  writeFileSync(authPath, JSON.stringify(data, null, 2), "utf-8")
    62	  chmodSync(authPath, 0o600)
    63	}

    65	function hasStoredBotToken(channel: RemoteChannel): boolean {
    66	  const data = readAuthData()
    67	  const providerId = AUTH_PROVIDER_IDS[channel]
    68	  const entry = data[providerId]
    69	  if (!entry) return false
    70	  // Could be a single credential or an array
    71	  const creds = Array.isArray(entry) ? entry : [entry]
    72	  return creds.some((c: unknown) => {
    73	    if (typeof c !== "object" || c === null) return false
    74	    const cred = c as Record<string, unknown>
    75	    return cred.type === "api_key" && typeof cred.key === "string" && cred.key.length > 0
    76	  })
    77	}

    79	function maskToken(token: string): string {
    80	  if (token.length <= 8) return token.slice(0, 2) + "***" + token.slice(-2)
    81	  return token.slice(0, 4) + "***" + token.slice(-4)
    82	}

    90	function clamp(value: number | undefined, defaultVal: number, min: number, max: number): number {
    91	  const v = typeof value === "number" && Number.isFinite(value) ? value : defaultVal
    92	  return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, v))

    95	function isValidChannel(ch: unknown): ch is RemoteChannel {
    96	  return typeof ch === "string" && (VALID_CHANNELS as readonly string[]).includes(ch)

    99	/**
   100	 * Parse YAML frontmatter from a markdown file.
   101	 * Uses the same indexOf-based approach as parsePreferencesMarkdown() in preferences.ts.
   102	 */
   103	function parseFrontmatter(content: string): { data: Record<string, unknown>; body: string; hasFrontmatter: boolean } {
   104	  const startMarker = content.startsWith("---\r\n") ? "---\r\n" : "---\n"
   105	  if (!content.startsWith(startMarker)) {
   106	    return { data: {}, body: content, hasFrontmatter: false }
   107	  }
   108	  const searchStart = startMarker.length
   109	  const endIdx = content.indexOf("\n---", searchStart)
   110	  if (endIdx === -1) {
   111	    return { data: {}, body: content, hasFrontmatter: false }
   112	  }
   113	  const block = content.slice(searchStart, endIdx)
   114	  const afterFrontmatter = content.slice(endIdx + 4) // skip \n---
   115	
   116	  try {
   117	    const parsed = parseYaml(block.replace(/\r/g, ""))
   118	    const data = typeof parsed === "object" && parsed !== null ? (parsed as Record<string, unknown>) : {}
   119	    return { data, body: afterFrontmatter, hasFrontmatter: true }
   120	  } catch {
   121	    return { data: {}, body: content, hasFrontmatter: false }
   122	  }
   123	}
   124	
   125	/**
   126	 * Write frontmatter data back to a markdown file, preserving the body content.
   127	 */
   128	function writeFrontmatter(data: Record<string, unknown>, body: string): string {
   129	  const yamlStr = stringifyYaml(data, { lineWidth: 0 }).trimEnd()
   130	  return `---\n${yamlStr}\n---${body}`
   131	}

   174	        envVarName: null,

   180	    }

   183	    if (!isValidChannel(channel)) {

   185	        config: null,
   186	        envVarSet: false,
   187	        tokenSet: false,

   189	        status: "invalid_channel",
   190	      }
   191	      return Response.json(response, {
   192	        headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" },
   193	      })
   194	    }
   195

   197	    const timeoutMinutes = clamp(rq.timeout_minutes as number | undefined, DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_MINUTES, MIN_TIMEOUT_MINUTES, MAX_TIMEOUT_MINUTES)
   198	    const pollIntervalSeconds = clamp(rq.poll_interval_seconds as number | undefined, DEFAULT_POLL_INTERVAL_SECONDS, MIN_POLL_INTERVAL_SECONDS, MAX_POLL_INTERVAL_SECONDS)
   199	    const envVarName = ENV_KEYS[channel]
   200	    const envVarSet = !!process.env[envVarName]
   201	    const tokenSet = hasStoredBotToken(channel) || envVarSet
   202	
   203	    const response: RemoteQuestionsResponse = {
   204	      config: {
   205	        channel,
   206	        channelId,
   207	        timeoutMinutes,
   208	        pollIntervalSeconds,
   209	      },
   210	      envVarSet,
   211	      tokenSet,
   212	      envVarName,
   213	      status: "configured",
   214	    }
   215	    return Response.json(response, {
   216	      headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" },
   217	    })
   218	  } catch (error) {
   219	    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
   220	    return Response.json(
   221	      { error: `Failed to read remote questions config: ${message}` },
   222	      { status: 500, headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },

   224	  }
   225	}

   228	
   229	export async function POST(request: Request): Promise<Response> {
   230	  try {
   231	    const body = await request.json() as Record<string, unknown>
   232	    const { channel, channelId, timeoutMinutes: rawTimeout, pollIntervalSeconds: rawPoll } = body as {
   233	      channel: unknown
   234	      channelId: unknown
   235	      timeoutMinutes: unknown
   236	      pollIntervalSeconds: unknown
   237	    }
   238

   240	    if (!isValidChannel(channel)) {

   242	        { error: `Invalid channel type: must be one of ${VALID_CHANNELS.join(", ")}` },
   243	        { status: 400, headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   244	      )
   245	    }
   246	
   247	    // Validate channelId
   248	    if (typeof channelId !== "string" || !channelId) {
   249	      return Response.json(
   250	        { error: "channelId is required and must be a non-empty string" },
   251	        { status: 400, headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   252	      )
   253	    }
   254	
   255	    if (!CHANNEL_ID_PATTERNS[channel].test(channelId)) {
   256	      return Response.json(
   257	        { error: `Invalid channel ID format for ${channel}. Expected pattern: ${CHANNEL_ID_PATTERNS[channel].source}` },
   258	        { status: 400, headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   259	      )
   260	    }
   261	
   262	    // Clamp timeout and poll interval
   263	    const timeoutMinutes = clamp(rawTimeout as number | undefined, DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_MINUTES, MIN_TIMEOUT_MINUTES, MAX_TIMEOUT_MINUTES)
   264	    const pollIntervalSeconds = clamp(rawPoll as number | undefined, DEFAULT_POLL_INTERVAL_SECONDS, MIN_POLL_INTERVAL_SECONDS, MAX_POLL_INTERVAL_SECONDS)
   265	
   266	    // Read current preferences
   267	    const prefsPath = getPreferencesPath()
   268	    let data: Record<string, unknown> = {}
   269	    let body2 = ""
   270	
   271	    if (existsSync(prefsPath)) {
   272	      const content = readFileSync(prefsPath, "utf-8")
   273	      const parsed = parseFrontmatter(content)
   274	      data = parsed.data
   275	      body2 = parsed.body
   276	    }
   277	
   278	    // Update remote_questions block
   279	    data.remote_questions = {
   280	      channel,
   281	      channel_id: channelId,
   282	      timeout_minutes: timeoutMinutes,
   283	      poll_interval_seconds: pollIntervalSeconds,
   284	    }
   285	
   286	    // Write back
   287	    const dir = dirname(prefsPath)
   288	    if (!existsSync(dir)) {
   289	      mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true })
   290	    }
   291	    writeFileSync(prefsPath, writeFrontmatter(data, body2), "utf-8")
   292	
   293	    return Response.json(
   294	      {
   295	        success: true,
   296	        config: { channel, channelId, timeoutMinutes, pollIntervalSeconds },
   297	      },
   298	      { headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   299	    )
   300	  } catch (error) {
   301	    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
   302	    return Response.json(
   303	      { error: `Failed to save remote questions config: ${message}` },
   304	      { status: 500, headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   305	    )
   306	  }
   307	}
   308	
   309	// ─── DELETE ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   310	
   311	export async function DELETE(): Promise<Response> {
   312	  try {
   313	    const prefsPath = getPreferencesPath()
   314	
   315	    if (!existsSync(prefsPath)) {
   316	      return Response.json(
   317	        { success: true },
   318	        { headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   319	      )
   320	    }
   321	
   322	    const content = readFileSync(prefsPath, "utf-8")
   323	    const { data, body, hasFrontmatter } = parseFrontmatter(content)
   324	
   325	    if (!hasFrontmatter || !data.remote_questions) {
   326	      return Response.json(
   327	        { success: true },
   328	        { headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   329	      )
   330	    }
   331	
   332	    delete data.remote_questions
   333	    writeFileSync(prefsPath, writeFrontmatter(data, body), "utf-8")
   334	
   335	    return Response.json(
   336	      { success: true },
   337	      { headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   338	    )
   339	  } catch (error) {
   340	    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
   341	    return Response.json(
   342	      { error: `Failed to remove remote questions config: ${message}` },
   343	      { status: 500, headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   344	    )
   345	  }
   346	}
   347	
   348	// ─── PATCH (save bot token) ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
   349	
   350	export async function PATCH(request: Request): Promise<Response> {
   351	  try {
   352	    const body = await request.json() as Record<string, unknown>
   353	    const { channel, token } = body as { channel: unknown; token: unknown }
   354	
   355	    if (!isValidChannel(channel)) {
   356	      return Response.json(
   357	        { error: `Invalid channel type: must be one of ${VALID_CHANNELS.join(", ")}` },
   358	        { status: 400, headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   359	      )
   360	    }
   361	
   362	    if (typeof token !== "string" || !token.trim()) {
   363	      return Response.json(
   364	        { error: "token is required and must be a non-empty string" },
   365	        { status: 400, headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   366	      )
   367	    }
   368	
   369	    const trimmedToken = token.trim()
   370	    const providerId = AUTH_PROVIDER_IDS[channel]
   371	
   372	    // Read existing auth data, merge the new credential
   373	    const authData = readAuthData()
   374	    const existingEntry = authData[providerId]
   375	    const existingCreds: unknown[] = existingEntry
   376	      ? (Array.isArray(existingEntry) ? existingEntry : [existingEntry])
   377	      : []
   378	
   379	    // Replace any existing api_key credential, keep OAuth
   380	    const oauthCreds = existingCreds.filter((c: unknown) => {
   381	      if (typeof c !== "object" || c === null) return false
   382	      return (c as Record<string, unknown>).type === "oauth"
   383	    })
   384	    const newCred = { type: "api_key", key: trimmedToken }
   385	    const merged = [...oauthCreds, newCred]
   386	    authData[providerId] = merged.length === 1 ? merged[0] : merged
   387	    writeAuthData(authData)
   388	
   389	    // Also set in process.env so it's available immediately
   390	    const envVar = ENV_KEYS[channel]
   391	    process.env[envVar] = trimmedToken
   392	
   393	    return Response.json(
   394	      { success: true, masked: maskToken(trimmedToken) },
   395	      { headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   396	    )
   397	  } catch (error) {
   398	    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)
   399	    return Response.json(
   400	      { error: `Failed to save bot token: ${message}` },
   401	      { status: 500, headers: { "Cache-Control": "no-store" } },
   402	    )
   403	  }
   404	}

    13	function getPreferencesPath(): string {
    14	  return join(homedir(), ".gsd", "preferences.md")

    16	
    17	function parseFrontmatter(content: string): { data: Record<string, unknown>; body: string } {
    18	  const startMarker = content.startsWith("---\r\n") ? "---\r\n" : "---\n"
    19	  if (!content.startsWith(startMarker)) return { data: {}, body: content }
    20	  const searchStart = startMarker.length
    21	  const endIdx = content.indexOf("\n---", searchStart)
    22	  if (endIdx === -1) return { data: {}, body: content }
    23	  const block = content.slice(searchStart, endIdx)
    24	  const afterFrontmatter = content.slice(endIdx + 4)
    25	  try {
    26	    const parsed = parseYaml(block.replace(/\r/g, ""))
    27	    const data = typeof parsed === "object" && parsed !== null ? (parsed as Record<string, unknown>) : {}
    28	    return { data, body: afterFrontmatter }
    29	  } catch {
    30	    return { data: {}, body: content }
    31	  }
    32	}
    33	
    34	function writeFrontmatter(data: Record<string, unknown>, body: string): string {
    35	  const yamlStr = stringifyYaml(data, { lineWidth: 0 }).trimEnd()
    36	  return `---\n${yamlStr}\n---${body}`
    37	}
    38	
    39	function readPrefs(): { data: Record<string, unknown>; body: string } {
    40	  const path = getPreferencesPath()
    41	  if (!existsSync(path)) return { data: {}, body: "\n" }
    42	  const content = readFileSync(path, "utf-8")
    43	  return parseFrontmatter(content)
    44	}
    45	
    46	function writePrefs(data: Record<string, unknown>, body: string): void {
    47	  const path = getPreferencesPath()
    48	  const dir = dirname(path)
    49	  if (!existsSync(dir)) mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true })
    50	  writeFileSync(path, writeFrontmatter(data, body), "utf-8")
    51	}

    72	export async function PATCH(request: Request): Promise<Response> {
    73	  try {
    74	    const body = await request.json() as Record<string, unknown>
    75	    const { flag, enabled } = body
    76	
    77	    const KNOWN_FLAGS = new Set(["rtk"])
    78	    if (typeof flag !== "string" || !KNOWN_FLAGS.has(flag)) {
    79	      return Response.json(
    80	        { error: `Unknown experimental flag "${flag}". Known flags: ${[...KNOWN_FLAGS].join(", ")}` },
    81	        { status: 400, headers: NO_STORE },
    82	      )
    83	    }
    84	    if (typeof enabled !== "boolean") {
    85	      return Response.json(

    95	      ? { ...(data.experimental as Record<string, unknown>) }
    96	      : {}
    97	    existing[flag] = enabled
    98	    data.experimental = existing
    99	
   100	    writePrefs(data, mdBody)
   101

   103	  } catch (err) {

   105	    return Response.json(

   107	      { status: 500, headers: NO_STORE },

   768	export async function ensurePreferencesFile(
   769	  path: string,
   770	  ctx: ExtensionCommandContext,
   771	  scope: "global" | "project",
   772	): Promise<void> {
   773	  if (!existsSync(path)) {
   774	    const template = await loadFile(join(dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url)), "templates", "preferences.md"));
   775	    if (!template) {
   776	      ctx.ui.notify("Could not load GSD preferences template.", "error");
   777	      return;
   778	    }
   779	    await saveFile(path, template);
   780	    ctx.ui.notify(`Created ${scope} GSD skill preferences at ${path}`, "info");
   781	  } else {
   782	    ctx.ui.notify(`Using existing ${scope} GSD skill preferences at ${path}`, "info");
   783	  }

Now let me think about edge cases:

1. **Migration path**: The loader checks `PREFERENCES.md` first, then falls back to `preferences.md`. This means existing projects with `preferences.md` will continue to work.

2. **New projects**: The init-wizard now creates `PREFERENCES.md`, so new projects will use the uppercase name.

3. **Writing preferences**: The `getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath()` and `getProjectGSDPreferencesPath()` now return the uppercase path. The `saveRemoteQuestionsConfig` in `remote-questions-config.ts` now uses uppercase. The web API routes check uppercase first, fall back to lowercase.

4. **Template file**: The template at `src/resources/extensions/gsd/templates/preferences.md` is a source resource, not the output file. It's loaded by `commands-prefs-wizard.ts` and used as content to populate new preference files. Since the target path is now uppercase (from `getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath()` / `getProjectGSDPreferencesPath()`), the template name doesn't matter.

5. **Detection**: Now checks uppercase first, falls back to lowercase.
